Had in like manner as to this shell so to bottles , bolts & other things such upon shipwracks , corallin matter & coralls have been found accreted . These observations serve to show that the manner of the production or as we vulgarly say the growth of corall is very litle different from that of the incrustata the Stalaginitæ & stalactite in the gritts & fissures of the rocks at land & in the Chanells of those call 'd petrifying waters .
